2.1.1.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:transaction-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:transaction-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:transaction-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:transaction-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:transaction-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.TransactionError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_TransactionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__TransactionError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_TransactionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    PkgMgrLog_notif_TransactionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_TransactionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.4.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:generic-notice/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:generic-notice/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:generic-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:generic-notice/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:generic-notice/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.GenericNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__GenericNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    PkgMgrLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.6.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-not-found/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-not-found/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-not-found/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-not-found/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-not-found/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.PackageNotFound.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_PackageNotFound_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__PackageNotFound__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.9.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:connection-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:connection-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:connection-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:connection-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:connection-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.ConnectionError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_ConnectionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__ConnectionError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_ConnectionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_ConnectionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.11.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:timeout-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:timeout-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:timeout-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:timeout-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:timeout-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.TimeoutError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_TimeoutError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__TimeoutError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_TimeoutError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    PkgMgrLog_notif_TimeoutError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_TimeoutError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.14.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:pkg-convert-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:pkg-convert-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:pkg-convert-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:pkg-convert-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:pkg-convert-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.PkgConvertError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_PkgConvertError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__PkgConvertError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_PkgConvertError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    PkgMgrLog_notif_PkgConvertError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_PkgConvertError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.16.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.PackageError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_PackageError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__PackageError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.19.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:image-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:image-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:image-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:image-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:image-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.ImageError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_ImageError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__ImageError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_ImageError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.21.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-catalog-update/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-catalog-update/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-catalog-update/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-catalog-update/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-catalog-update/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.PackageCatalogUpdate.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_PackageCatalogUpdate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__PackageCatalogUpdate__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.24.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-file-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-file-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:package-file-delete/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-file-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:package-file-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.PackageFileDelete.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_PackageFileDelete_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__PackageFileDelete__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_PackageFileDelete_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.26.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-add/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-add/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-add/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-add/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-add/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.NsdCatalogAdd.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_NsdCatalogAdd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__NsdCatalogAdd__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_NsdCatalogAdd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    PkgMgrLog_notif_NsdCatalogAdd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_NsdCatalogAdd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.28.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-delete/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:nsd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.NsdCatalogDelete.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_NsdCatalogDelete_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__NsdCatalogDelete__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_NsdCatalogDelete_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.31.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:vnfd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:vnfd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:vnfd-catalog-delete/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:vnfd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:vnfd-catalog-delete/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.VnfdCatalogDelete.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_VnfdCatalogDelete_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__VnfdCatalogDelete__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_VnfdCatalogDelete_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_VnfdCatalogDelete_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.33.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-failure/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-failure/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-failure/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:export-failure/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:export-failure/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.ExportFailure.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_ExportFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__ExportFailure__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.36.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-to-ro-misc-multiple/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-to-ro-misc-multiple/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-to-ro-misc-multiple/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:export-to-ro-misc-multiple/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:export-to-ro-misc-multiple/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.ExportToRoMiscMultiple.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_ExportToRoMiscMultiple_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__ExportToRoMiscMultiple__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.38.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-success/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-success/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:export-success/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:export-success/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:export-success/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.ExportSuccess.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_ExportSuccess_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__ExportSuccess__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.41.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:account-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:account-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:account-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:account-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:account-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.AccountDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_AccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__AccountDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_AccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier

2.1.43.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:catalog-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:catalog-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:catalog-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:catalog-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:catalog-debug/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.CatalogDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_CatalogDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__CatalogDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_CatalogDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.46.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:yang-transaltion-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:yang-transaltion-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:yang-transaltion-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:yang-transaltion-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:yang-transaltion-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.YangTransaltionError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_YangTransaltionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__YangTransaltionError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.48.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:name-not-in-descriptor/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:name-not-in-descriptor/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:name-not-in-descriptor/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:name-not-in-descriptor/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:name-not-in-descriptor/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.NameNotInDescriptor.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_NameNotInDescriptor_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__NameNotInDescriptor__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_NameNotInDescriptor_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    PkgMgrLog_notif_NameNotInDescriptor_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_NameNotInDescriptor_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.50.1.3  container pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:datastore-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:datastore-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /pkg-mgr-log:datastore-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:datastore-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/pkg-mgr-log:datastore-error/pkg-mgr-log:template_params/pkg-mgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .pkg_mgr_log.YangNotif.PkgMgrLog.DatastoreError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    PkgMgrLogYang.YangNotif_PkgMgrLog_DatastoreError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    PkgMgrLog__YangNotif__PkgMgrLog__DatastoreError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_DatastoreError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    PkgMgrLog_notif_DatastoreError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_PkgMgrLog_PkgMgrLog_notif_DatastoreError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
